### Round 16: Russian Grand Prix

### Round 20: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 2019-11-17*

#### Qualifying ELO Changes

| Driver | Constructor | Position | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | Result | vs Teammate |
